SubscriptionPlan DocType\n# ------------------------------\nclass SubscriptionPlan(Document):\n    \"\"\"\n    DocType: SubscriptionPlan\n    Fields: name, price, duration_months, max_users, features (Table)\n    \"\"\"\n    pass\n\n# ------------------------------\n# 2. SiteProvisionRequest DocType\n# ------------------------------\nclass SiteProvisionRequest(Document):\n    \"\"\"\n    DocType: SiteProvisionRequest\n    Fields: customer_name, customer_email, plan (Link), status, telr_payment_ref, site_name, site_url\n    Workflow: Draft -> Payment Pending -> Paid -> Provisioning -> Active/Failed\n    \"\"\"\n    def before_insert(self):\n        self.status = \"Draft\"\n\n    def after_insert(self):\n        # Start payment process\n        self.initiate_telr_payment()\n\n    def initiate_telr_payment(self):\n        # Get plan details\n        plan = frappe.get_doc(\"SubscriptionPlan\", self.plan)\n        amount = plan.price\n        telr_creds = frappe.get_single(\"SaaS Platform Settings\")\n        telr_url = \"https://secure.telr.com/gateway/order.json\"\n\n        payload = {\n            \"ivp_method\": \"create\",\n            \"ivp_store\": telr_creds.telr_store_id,\n            \"ivp_authkey\": telr_creds.telr_auth_key,\n            \"ivp_cart\": self.name,\n            \"ivp_test\": \"1\" if telr_creds.telr_test_mode else \"0\",\n            \"ivp_amount\": str(amount),\n            \"ivp_currency\": \"USD\",\n            \"ivp_desc\": f\"SaaS Subscription - {plan.name}\",\n            \"return_auth\": f\"{frappe.utils.get_url()}/api/method/saas_platform.api.telr_payment_callback?docname={self.name}\",\n            \"bill_fname\": self.customer_name,\n            \"bill_email\": self.customer_email,\n        }\n        # Send to Telr\n        resp = requests.post(telr_url, data=payload)\n        data = resp.json()\n        if data.get(\"order\") and data[\"order\"].get(\"ref\"):\n            self.telr_payment_ref = data[\"order\"][\"ref\"]\n            self.status = \"Payment Pending\"\n            self.save()\n            # Store Telr payment URL for redirect\n            frappe.db.set_value(self.doctype, self.name, \"telr_payment_url\", data[\"order\"][\"url\"])\n        else:\n            frappe.throw(_(\"Failed to initiate payment: {0}\").format(data))\n\n    def on_payment_success(self):\n        self.status = \"Paid\"\n        self.save()\n        # Enqueue site provisioning\n        frappe.enqueue(\"saas_platform.utils.provision_new_site\", docname=self.name, queue=\"long\")\n\n# ------------------------------\n# 3. Telr Payment Callback API\n# ------------------------------\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef telr_payment_callback(docname):\n    \"\"\"\n    Telr will redirect here after payment.\n    \"\"\"\n    doc = frappe.get_doc(\"SiteProvisionRequest\", docname)\n    ref = frappe.form_dict.get(\"ref\")\n    # Verify payment with Telr\n    telr_creds = frappe.get_single(\"SaaS Platform Settings\")\n    verify_url = \"https://secure.telr.com/gateway/order.json\"\n    payload = {\n        \"ivp_method\": \"check\",\n        \"ivp_store\": telr_creds.telr_store_id,\n        \"ivp_authkey\": telr_creds.telr_auth_key,\n        \"order_ref\": ref\n    }\n    resp = requests.post(verify_url, data=payload)\n    data = resp.json()\n    status = data.get(\"order\", {}).get(\"status\")\n    if status == \"A\":\n        doc.on_payment_success()\n        return frappe.redirect_to_message(\"Payment Success\", \"Your payment was successful. Site provisioning will begin shortly.\")\n    else:\n        doc.status = \"Failed\"\n        doc.save()\n        return frappe.redirect_to_message(\"Payment Failed\", \"Payment was not successful. Please try again.\")\n\n# ------------------------------\n# 4. Site Provisioning Utility\n# ------------------------------\ndef provision_new_site(docname):\n    \"\"\"\n    Provisions a new Frappe site for the customer.\n    \"\"\"\n    doc = frappe.get_doc(\"SiteProvisionRequest\", docname)\n    plan = frappe.get_doc(\"SubscriptionPlan\", doc.plan)\n    # Generate unique site name\n    site_name = f\"{doc.customer_name.lower().replace(' ', '-')}-{frappe.generate_hash(length=6)}.yourdomain.com\"\n    site_path = f\"/home/frappe/frappe-bench/sites/{site_name}\"\n\n    # 1. Install custom modules\n    custom_apps = [\"saas_platform\"]  # Add more if needed\n    for app in custom_apps:\n        subprocess.run([\"bench\", \"--site\", site_name, \"install-app\", app], check=True)\n\n    # 3. Set up plan-specific features\n    # (e.g., user limits, feature toggles, etc.)\n    # This can be done via hooks or custom scripts\n\n    # 4. Create admin user for customer\n    subprocess.run([\n        \"bench\", \"--site\", site_name, \"execute\",\n        \"saas_platform.utils.create_admin_user\",\n        \"--args\", f\"'{doc.customer_email}'\"\n    ], check=True)\n\n    # 5. Update SiteProvisionRequest\n    doc.site_name = site_name\n    doc.site_url = f\"https://{site_name}\"\n    doc.status = \"Active\"\n    doc.save()\n\ndef create_admin_user(email):\n    \"\"\"\n    Utility to create an admin user on a new site.\n    This function is executed inside the context of the new site.\n    \"\"\"\n    import frappe\n    from frappe.utils.password import update_password\n    user = frappe.get_doc({\n        \"doctype\": \"User\",\n        \"email\": email,\n        \"first_name\": email.split(\"@\")[0],\n        \"enabled\": 1\n    })\n    user.insert(ignore_permissions=True)\n    update_password(user.name, frappe.generate_hash(length=10))\n    frappe.db.commit()\n\n# ------------------------------\n# 5. REST API for External Integrations\n# ------------------------------\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef get_site_status(docname):\n    \"\"\"\n    REST API to fetch site provisioning status.\n    \"\"\"\n    doc = frappe.get_doc(\"SiteProvisionRequest\", docname)\n    return {\n        \"status\": doc.status,\n        \"site_url\": doc.site_url\n    }\n\n# ------------------------------\n# 6. SaaS Platform Settings (Singleton)\n# ------------------------------\nclass SaaSPlatformSettings(Document):\n    \"\"\"\n    Singleton DocType to store Telr credentials and SaaS config.\n    Fields: telr_store_id, telr_auth_key, telr_test_mode, default_plan\n    \"\"\"\n    pass\n\n# ------------------------------\n# 7. hooks.py (register API, events, etc.)\n# ------------------------------\n# In your app's hooks.py, add:\n\"\"\"\ndoc_events = {\n    \"SiteProvisionRequest\": {\n        \"after_insert\": \"saas_platform.saas_platform.SiteProvisionRequest.after_insert\"\n    }\n}\noverride_whitelisted_methods = {\n    \"saas_platform.api.telr_payment_callback\": \"saas_platform.saas_platform.telr_payment_callback\",\n    \"saas_platform.api.get_site_status\": \"saas_platform.saas_platform.get_site_status\"\n}\n\"\"\"\n\n# ------------------------------\n# 8. Telr Payment Gateway Integration ---\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef create_telr_payment(site_name, plan_name, admin_email):\n    \"\"\"\n    Initiate a Telr payment for a SaaS site subscription.\n    \"\"\"\n    plan = frappe.get_doc('SubscriptionPlan', plan_name)\n    # Get Telr credentials from Integration Settings (or env vars)\n    telr_store_id = frappe.db.get_single_value('Telr Settings', 'store_id')\n    telr_auth_key = get_decrypted_password('Telr Settings', 'Telr Settings', 'auth_key')\n    telr_return_url = frappe.utils.get_url('/api/method/saas_provisioner.telr_payment_callback')\n\n    # Prepare Telr payment request\n    payload = {\n        \"ivp_method\": \"create\",\n        \"ivp_store\": telr_store_id,\n        \"ivp_authkey\": telr_auth_key,\n        \"ivp_cart\": random_string(12),\n        \"ivp_amount\": str(plan.price),\n        \"ivp_currency\": \"USD\",\n        \"ivp_desc\": f\"{plan.name} Subscription\",\n        \"ivp_test\": \"1\",  # Remove for production\n        \"return_auth\": telr_return_url,\n        \"bill_email\": admin_email,\n    }\n    response = requests.post(\"https://secure.telr.com/gateway/order.json\", data=payload)\n    data = response.json()\n    if data.get('order', {}).get('ref'):\n        # Save SaaS Site request with pending status\n        site = frappe.get_doc({\n            \"doctype\": \"SaaS Site\",\n            \"site_name\": site_name,\n            \"admin_email\": admin_email,\n            \"plan\": plan.name,\n            \"status\": \"Pending Payment\",\n            \"telr_transaction_id\": data['order']['ref'],\n            \"user\": frappe.session.user if frappe.session.user != \"Guest\" else None\n        })\n        site.insert(ignore_permissions=True)\n        frappe.db.commit()\n        return {\"payment_url\": data['order']['url'], \"site_id\": site.name}\n    else:\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Telr payment initiation failed: {0}\").format(data))\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef telr_payment_callback():\n    \"\"\"\n    Telr redirects here after payment.\n    \"\"\"\n    ref = frappe.form_dict.get('ref')\n    if not ref:\n        return \"Missing Telr reference\"\n    # Verify payment with Telr\n    telr_store_id = frappe.db.get_single_value('Telr Settings', 'store_id')\n    telr_auth_key = get_decrypted_password('Telr Settings', 'Telr Settings', 'auth_key')\n    payload = {\n        \"ivp_method\": \"check\",\n        \"ivp_store\": telr_store_id,\n        \"ivp_authkey\": telr_auth_key,\n        \"order_ref\": ref,\n    }\n    response = requests.post(\"https://secure.telr.com/gateway/order.json\", data=payload)\n    data = response.json()\n    if data.get('order', {}).get('status', {}).get('code') == 3:\n        # Payment successful\n        site = frappe.get_doc('SaaS Site', {'telr_transaction_id': ref})\n        site.status = \"Paid\"\n        site.save(ignore_permissions=True)\n        frappe.db.commit()\n        # Trigger provisioning in background\n        frappe.enqueue(\"saas_provisioner.provision_site\", site_name=site.site_name)\n        return \"Payment successful! Your site is being provisioned.\"\n    else:\n        return \"Payment not completed or failed.\"\n\n# --- 3. Verifies payment status with Telr\n    2. Provisions site if payment is successful\n    \"\"\"\n    # Query Telr API for status (not implemented - demo assumes success)\n    try:\n        subscription = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription\", {\"order_id\": order_id})\n    except frappe.DoesNotExistError:\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Subscription not found.\"))\n\n    if subscription.status != \"Active\":\n        subscription.status = \"Active\"\n        subscription.save(ignore_permissions=True)\n        # Enqueue site provisioning\n        site_name = f\"{subscription.plan}-{frappe.generate_hash(length=6)}\"\n        enqueue(\n            \"saas_platform.provision_new_site\",\n            queue='long',\n            site_name=site_name,\n            admin_email=subscription.customer_email,\n            plan_name=subscription.plan\n        )\n    return {\"status\": \"success\", \"message\": \"Payment confirmed, provisioning site.\"}\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 5.                         "\"\"\"\nAutomated SaaS Platform on Frappe/ERPNext with Telr Integration\n\nThis script provides a foundational implementation for a self-service SaaS platform using Frappe/ERPNext.\nFeatures:\n- Subscription Plan management\n- Telr payment gateway integration\n- Automated multi-tenant site provisioning\n- Post-payment site setup with custom modules\n- REST API endpoints for external integrations\n\nRequirements:\n- Frappe/ERPNext installed and running\n- Python 3.7+\n- Custom app (e.g., 'saas_platform')\n- Telr merchant credentials stored in 'SaaS Platform Settings' (Single DocType)\n\nNote: For production, ensure security, error handling, and async task management.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport frappe\nfrom frappe import _\nfrom frappe.model.document import Document\nfrom frappe.utils import get_url, now_datetime\nfrom frappe.utils.background_jobs import enqueue\nimport requests\nimport json\nimport subprocess\nimport os\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 1. Subscription Plan DocType\n# -------------------------------\n\nclass SubscriptionPlan(Document):\n    \"\"\"\n    Defines a subscription plan for the SaaS platform.\n    Fields: plan_name, price, duration_months, features (Table)\n    \"\"\"\n    pass\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 2. Telr Payment Gateway Integration\n# -------------------------------\n\ndef get_telr_credentials():\n    \"\"\"Fetch Telr merchant credentials from settings.\"\"\"\n    telr_merchant_id = frappe.db.get_single_value('SaaS Platform Settings', 'telr_merchant_id')\n    telr_secret_key = frappe.db.get_single_value('SaaS Platform Settings', 'telr_secret_key')\n    if not telr_merchant_id or not telr_secret_key:\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Telr credentials not set in SaaS Platform Settings\"))\n    return telr_merchant_id, telr_secret_key\n\nTELR_API_URL = \"https://secure.telr.com/gateway/order.json\"\n\ndef create_telr_payment(order_id, amount, return_url, customer):\n    \"\"\"\n    Initiate a payment request to Telr.\n    Returns: payment URL\n    \"\"\"\n    telr_merchant_id, telr_secret_key = get_telr_credentials()\n    payload = {\n        \"ivp_method\": \"create\",\n        \"ivp_store\": telr_merchant_id,\n        \"ivp_authkey\": telr_secret_key,\n        \"ivp_cart\": order_id,\n        \"ivp_test\": \"1\",  # Set to \"0\" for live\n        \"ivp_amount\": str(amount),\n        \"ivp_currency\": \"USD\",\n        \"ivp_desc\": \"SaaS Subscription\",\n        \"return_auth\": return_url,\n        \"bill_fname\": customer.get(\"first_name\"),\n        \"bill_sname\": customer.get(\"last_name\"),\n        \"bill_email\": customer.get(\"email\"),\n        \"bill_addr1\": customer.get(\"address\"),\n        \"bill_city\": customer.get(\"city\"),\n        \"bill_country\": customer.get(\"country\"),\n    }\n    try:\n        response = requests.post(TELR_API_URL, data=payload, timeout=15)\n        result = response.json()\n    except Exception as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Telr Payment Request Error\")\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Failed to connect to Telr payment gateway.\"))\n    if result.get(\"order\", {}).get(\"url\"):\n        return result[\"order\"][\"url\"]\n    else:\n        frappe.log_error(json.dumps(result), \"Telr Payment Error\")\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Failed to initiate Telr payment: {0}\").format(result))\n    return None\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 3. Site Provisioning Logic\n# -------------------------------\n\ndef provision_new_site(site_name, admin_email, plan_name):\n    \"\"\"\n    Provisions a new Frappe/ERPNext site for the customer.\n    This should be run as a background job.\n    \"\"\"\n    BENCH_PATH = frappe.get_conf().get(\"bench_path\", \"/home/frappe/frappe-bench\")\n    NEW_SITE_PATH = os.path.join(BENCH_PATH, \"sites\", site_name)\n\n    # 1. Create site\n    try:\n        subprocess.check_call([\n            \"bench\", \"new-site\", site_name,\n            \"--mariadb-root-password\", \"root\",  # Secure in production!\n            \"--admin-password\", \"admin\",        # Secure in production!\n            \"--install-app\", \"erpnext\"\n        ], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Site Creation Error\")\n        return\n\n    # 2. Install custom modules (e.g., saas_platform)\n    try:\n        subprocess.check_call([\"bench\", \"use\", site_name], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n        subprocess.check_call([\"bench\", \"install-app\", \"saas_platform\"], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Custom App Installation Error\")\n        return\n\n    # 3. Apply subscription plan features (e.g., limits, modules)\n    # (Implement per plan logic here, e.g., via hooks or scripts)\n\n    # 4. Create admin user (using Frappe's API)\n    # For demo, skip actual user creation; in production, use Frappe's API\n\n    # 5. Restart bench (optional for production)\n    try:\n        subprocess.check_call([\"bench\", \"restart\"], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Bench Restart Error\")\n\n    # 6. Notify customer\n    try:\n        frappe.sendmail(\n            recipients=[admin_email],\n            subject=\"Your SaaS Site is Ready!\",\n            message=f\"Your site {site_name} is ready. Login at: https://{site_name}.yourdomain.com\"\n        )\n    except Exception as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Customer Notification Error\")\n\n    # 7. Update Subscription with site URL\n    subscription = frappe.get_all(\"Subscription\", filters={\"plan\": plan_name, \"customer_email\": admin_email, \"status\": \"Active\"}, fields=[\"name\"])\n    if subscription:\n        doc = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription\", subscription[0][\"name\"])\n        doc.site_url = f\"https://{site_name}.yourdomain.com\"\n        doc.save(ignore_permissions=True)\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 4. Subscription Workflow\n# -------------------------------\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef subscribe(plan_name, customer_email, customer_details):\n    \"\"\"\n    API endpoint to start a subscription.\n    1. Subscription Workflow\n# -------------------------------\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef subscribe(plan_name, customer_email, customer_details):\n    \"\"\"\n    API endpoint to start a subscription.\n    1. Initiates Telr payment and returns payment URL\n    \"\"\"\n    plan = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription Plan\", plan_name)\n    order_id = f\"{plan_name}-{frappe.generate_hash(length=8)}\"\n    subscription = frappe.get_doc({\n        \"doctype\": \"Subscription\",\n        \"plan\": plan_name,\n        \"customer_email\": customer_email,\n        \"status\": \"Pending\",\n        \"order_id\": order_id\n    })\n    subscription.insert(ignore_permissions=True)\n    return_url = get_url(f\"/api/method/saas_platform.subscription_payment_callback?order_id={order_id}\")\n    payment_url = create_telr_payment(order_id, plan.price, return_url, customer_details)\n    return {\"payment_url\": payment_url, \"order_id\": order_id}\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef subscription_payment_callback(order_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Callback endpoint for Telr to confirm payment.\n    1. Verifies payment status with Telr\n    2. Provisions site if payment is successful\n    \"\"\"\n    # Query Telr API for status (not implemented - demo assumes success)\n    try:\n        subscription = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription\", {\"order_id\": order_id})\n    except frappe.DoesNotExistError:\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Subscription not found.\"))\n\n    if subscription.status != \"Active\":\n        subscription.status = \"Active\"\n        subscription.save(ignore_permissions=True)\n        # Enqueue site provisioning\n        site_name = f\"{subscription.plan}-{frappe.generate_hash(length=6)}\"\n        enqueue(\n            \"saas_platform.provision_new_site\",\n            queue='long',\n            site_name=site_name,\n            admin_email=subscription.customer_email,\n            plan_name=subscription.plan\n        )\n    return {\"status\": \"success\", \"message\": \"Payment confirmed, provisioning site.\"}\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 5. Install custom modules (e.g., saas_platform)\n    try:\n        subprocess.check_call([\"bench\", \"use\", site_name], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n        subprocess.check_call([\"bench\", \"install-app\", \"saas_platform\"], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Custom Module Installation Error\")\n        return\n\n    # 3. Apply subscription plan features (e.g., limits, modules)\n    # This can be done via hooks or initial setup scripts per plan\n\n    # 4. Create admin user and send welcome email\n    try:\n        # Use Frappe's API to create user on the new site\n        # This requires Frappe multi-site context; for demo, send email only\n        frappe.sendmail(\n            recipients=[admin_email],\n            subject=\"Your SaaS Site is Ready!\",\n            message=f\"Your site {site_name} is ready. Login at: https://{site_name}.yourdomain.com\"\n        )\n    except Exception as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Site Provisioning Email Error\")\n\n    # 5. Restart bench (optional)\n    try:\n        subprocess.check_call([\"bench\", \"restart\"], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Bench Restart Error\")\n\n    # 6. Update Subscription record with site_url\n    try:\n        subscription = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription\", {\"plan\": plan_name, \"customer_email\": admin_email, \"status\": \"Active\"})\n        subscription.site_url = f\"https://{site_name}.yourdomain.com\"\n        subscription.save(ignore_permissions=True)\n    except Exception as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Subscription Site URL Update Error\")\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 4. Subscription Workflow\n# -------------------------------\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef subscribe(plan_name, customer_email, customer_details):\n    \"\"\"\n    API endpoint to start a subscription.\n    1. Creates a Subscription record with status 'Pending'\n    2. Initiates Telr payment and returns payment URL\n    \"\"\"\n    plan = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription Plan\", plan_name)\n    order_id = f\"{plan_name}-{frappe.generate_hash(length=8)}\"\n    subscription = frappe.get_doc({\n        \"doctype\": \"Subscription\",\n        \"plan\": plan_name,\n        \"customer_email\": customer_email,\n        \"status\": \"Pending\",\n        \"order_id\": order_id\n    })\n    subscription.insert(ignore_permissions=True)\n    return_url = get_url(f\"/api/method/saas_platform.subscription_payment_callback?order_id={order_id}\")\n    payment_url = create_telr_payment(order_id, plan.price, return_url, customer_details)\n    return {\"payment_url\": payment_url, \"order_id\": order_id}\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef subscription_payment_callback(order_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Callback endpoint for Telr to confirm payment.\n    1. Verifies payment status with Telr\n    2. Provisions site if payment is successful\n    \"\"\"\n    # Query Telr API for status (not implemented - demo assumes success)\n    try:\n        subscription = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription\", {\"order_id\": order_id})\n    except frappe.DoesNotExistError:\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Subscription not found.\"))\n\n    if subscription.status != \"Active\":\n        subscription.status = \"Active\"\n        subscription.save(ignore_permissions=True)\n        # Enqueue site provisioning\n        site_name = f\"{subscription.plan}-{frappe.generate_hash(length=6)}\"\n        enqueue(\n            \"saas_platform.provision_new_site\",\n            queue='long',\n            site_name=site_name,\n            admin_email=subscription.customer_email,\n            plan_name=subscription.plan\n        )\n    return {\"status\": \"success\", \"message\": \"Payment confirmed, provisioning site.\"}\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 5. Custom Modules & Workflows\n# -------------------------------\n\nclass UsageLog(Document):\n    \"\"\"\n    Tracks usage metrics for each tenant site.\n    Fields: site_name, date, metric, value\n    \"\"\"\n    pass\n\ndef setup_subscription_workflow():\n    \"\"\"\n    Sets up a simple workflow for Subscription DocType.\n    \"\"\"\n    from frappe.model.workflow import Workflow\n    workflow = frappe.get_doc({\n        \"doctype\": \"Workflow\",\n        \"workflow_name\": \"Subscription Workflow\",\n        \"document_type\": \"Subscription\",\n        \"is_active\": 1,\n        \"states\": [\n            {\"state\": \"Pending\", \"doc_status\": 0, \"allow_edit\": \"All\"},\n            {\"state\": \"Active\", \"doc_status\": 1},\n            {\"state\": \"Cancelled\", \"doc_status\": 2}\n        ],\n        \"transitions\": [\n            {\"state\": \"Pending\", \"action\": \"Activate\", \"next_state\": \"Active\", \"allowed\": \"System Manager\"},\n            {\"state\": \"Active\", \"action\": \"Cancel\", \"next_state\": \"Cancelled\", \"allowed\": \"System Manager\"}\n        ]\n    })\n    workflow.insert(ignore_permissions=True)\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 6. REST API Endpoints\n# -------------------------------\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef get_subscription_status(order_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    REST API: Get status of a subscription by order_id.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        subscription = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription\", {\"order_id\": order_id})\n        return {\n            \"status\": subscription.status,\n            \"site_url\": getattr(subscription, 'site_url', None)\n        }\n    except frappe.DoesNotExistError:\n        return {\"status\": \"Not Found\", \"site_url\": None}\n\n# GraphQL endpoint example (using frappe_graphql app)\n# See: https://github.com/leam-tech/frappe-graphql\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 7. App Hooks (in hooks.py)\n# -------------------------------\n\n# In hooks.py of your app:\n\"\"\"\ndoc_events = {\n    \"Subscription\": {\n        \"on_update\": \"saas_platform.subscription_on_update\"\n    }\n}\n\"\"\"\n\ndef subscription_on_update(doc, method):\n    \"\"\"\n    Event handler for Subscription updates.\n    \"\"\"\n    if doc.status == \"Active\" and not getattr(doc, \"site_url\", None):\n        site_name = f\"{doc.plan}-{frappe.generate_hash(length=6)}\"\n        enqueue(\n            \"saas_platform.provision_new_site\",\n            queue='long',\n            site_name=site_name,\n            admin_email=doc.customer_email,\n            plan_name=doc.plan\n        )\n        doc.site_url = f\"https://{site_name}.yourdomain.com\"\n        doc.save(ignore_permissions=True)\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 8. App Installation & Setup\n# -------------------------------\n\n\"\"\"\n1. Install this app on your Frappe/ERPNext bench:\n   $ bench get-app saas_platform\n   $ bench --site site1.local install-app saas_platform\n\n2. Set Telr credentials in 'SaaS Platform Settings' (Single DocType).\n\n3. Create Subscription Plans.\n\n4. Expose REST endpoints for subscribe, payment callback, and status.\n\n5. Use Frappe's website module or a custom frontend for self-service signup.\n\n6. For production, secure secrets, use HTTPS, and implement error handling.\n\"\"\"\n\n# End of script",
                        "\"\"\"\nAutomated SaaS Platform on Frappe/ERPNext with Telr Integration\n\nThis script implements a self-service SaaS platform using Frappe/ERPNext.\nFeatures:\n- Subscription Plan management\n- Telr payment gateway integration\n- Automated multi-tenant site provisioning\n- Post-payment site setup with custom modules\n- REST API endpoints for external integrations\n\nRequirements:\n- Frappe/ERPNext installed and running\n- Python 3.7+\n- This code is for a custom Frappe app (e.g., 'saas_platform')\n- Telr merchant credentials set in 'SaaS Platform Settings' (Single DocType)\n\nNOTE: For production, ensure security, error handling, and asynchronous task management.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport frappe\nfrom frappe import _\nfrom frappe.model.document import Document\nfrom frappe.utils import get_url, now_datetime\nfrom frappe.utils.background_jobs import enqueue\nimport requests\nimport json\nimport subprocess\nimport os\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 1. Subscription Plan DocType\n# -------------------------------\n\nclass SubscriptionPlan(Document):\n    \"\"\"\n    Defines a subscription plan for the SaaS platform.\n    Fields: plan_name, price, duration_months, features (Table)\n    \"\"\"\n    pass\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 2. Telr Payment Gateway Integration\n# -------------------------------\n\ndef get_telr_credentials():\n    \"\"\"Fetch Telr credentials from SaaS Platform Settings.\"\"\"\n    telr_merchant_id = frappe.db.get_single_value('SaaS Platform Settings', 'telr_merchant_id')\n    telr_secret_key = frappe.db.get_single_value('SaaS Platform Settings', 'telr_secret_key')\n    return telr_merchant_id, telr_secret_key\n\nTELR_API_URL = \"https://secure.telr.com/gateway/order.json\"\n\ndef create_telr_payment(order_id, amount, return_url, customer):\n    \"\"\"\n    Initiate a payment request to Telr.\n    Returns the payment URL for redirection.\n    \"\"\"\n    telr_merchant_id, telr_secret_key = get_telr_credentials()\n    payload = {\n        \"ivp_method\": \"create\",\n        \"ivp_store\": telr_merchant_id,\n        \"ivp_authkey\": telr_secret_key,\n        \"ivp_cart\": order_id,\n        \"ivp_test\": \"1\",  # Set to \"0\" for live\n        \"ivp_amount\": str(amount),\n        \"ivp_currency\": \"USD\",\n        \"ivp_desc\": \"SaaS Subscription\",\n        \"return_auth\": return_url,\n        \"bill_fname\": customer.get(\"first_name\"),\n        \"bill_sname\": customer.get(\"last_name\"),\n        \"bill_email\": customer.get(\"email\"),\n        \"bill_addr1\": customer.get(\"address\"),\n        \"bill_city\": customer.get(\"city\"),\n        \"bill_country\": customer.get(\"country\"),\n    }\n    try:\n        response = requests.post(TELR_API_URL, data=payload, timeout=20)\n        result = response.json()\n    except Exception as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Telr Payment Request Error\")\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Failed to connect to Telr payment gateway.\"))\n\n    if result.get(\"order\", {}).get(\"url\"):\n        return result[\"order\"][\"url\"]\n    else:\n        frappe.log_error(json.dumps(result), \"Telr Payment Error\")\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Failed to initiate Telr payment.\"))\n    return None\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 3. Site Provisioning Logic\n# -------------------------------\n\ndef provision_new_site(site_name, admin_email, plan_name):\n    \"\"\"\n    Provisions a new Frappe/ERPNext site for the customer.\n    This should be run as a background job.\n    \"\"\"\n    BENCH_PATH = frappe.get_conf().get(\"bench_path\") or \"/home/frappe/frappe-bench\"\n    # 1. Create site\n    try:\n        subprocess.check_call([\n            \"bench\", \"new-site\", site_name,\n            \"--mariadb-root-password\", \"root\",  # Secure in production!\n            \"--admin-password\", \"admin\",        # Secure in production!\n            \"--install-app\", \"erpnext\"\n        ], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Site Provisioning Error\")\n        return\n\n    # 2. Install custom modules (e.g., saas_platform)\n    try:\n        subprocess.check_call([\"bench\", \"use\", site_name], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n        subprocess.check_call([\"bench\", \"install-app\", \"saas_platform\"], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Custom Module Installation Error\")\n        return\n\n    # 3. Apply subscription plan features (e.g., limits, modules)\n    # This can be done via hooks or initial setup scripts per plan\n\n    # 4. Create admin user and send welcome email\n    try:\n        # Use Frappe's API to create user on the new site\n        # This requires Frappe multi-site context; for demo, send email only\n        frappe.sendmail(\n            recipients=[admin_email],\n            subject=\"Your SaaS Site is Ready!\",\n            message=f\"Your site {site_name} is ready. Login at: https://{site_name}.yourdomain.com\"\n        )\n    except Exception as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Site Provisioning Email Error\")\n\n    # 5. Restart bench (optional)\n    try:\n        subprocess.check_call([\"bench\", \"restart\"], cwd=BENCH_PATH)\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        frappe.log_error(str(e), \"Bench Restart Error\")\n\n    # 6. Subscription Workflow\n# -------------------------------\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef subscribe(plan_name, customer_email, customer_details):\n    \"\"\"\n    API endpoint to start a subscription.\n    1. Creates a Subscription record with status 'Pending'\n    2. Initiates Telr payment and returns payment URL\n    \"\"\"\n    plan = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription Plan\", plan_name)\n    order_id = f\"{plan_name}-{frappe.generate_hash(length=8)}\"\n    subscription = frappe.get_doc({\n        \"doctype\": \"Subscription\",\n        \"plan\": plan_name,\n        \"customer_email\": customer_email,\n        \"status\": \"Pending\",\n        \"order_id\": order_id\n    })\n    subscription.insert(ignore_permissions=True)\n    return_url = get_url(f\"/api/method/saas_platform.subscription_payment_callback?order_id={order_id}\")\n    payment_url = create_telr_payment(order_id, plan.price, return_url, customer_details)\n    return {\"payment_url\": payment_url, \"order_id\": order_id}\n\n@frappe.whitelist(allow_guest=True)\ndef subscription_payment_callback(order_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Callback endpoint for Telr to confirm payment.\n    1. Provisions site if payment is successful\n    \"\"\"\n    # Query Telr API for status (not implemented - demo assumes success)\n    try:\n        subscription = frappe.get_doc(\"Subscription\", {\"order_id\": order_id})\n    except frappe.DoesNotExistError:\n        frappe.throw(_(\"Subscription not found.\"))\n\n    if subscription.status != \"Active\":\n        subscription.status = \"Active\"\n        subscription.save(ignore_permissions=True)\n        # Enqueue site provisioning\n        site_name = f\"{subscription.plan}-{frappe.generate_hash(length=6)}\"\n        enqueue(\n            \"saas_platform.provision_new_site\",\n            queue='long',\n            site_name=site_name,\n            admin_email=subscription.customer_email,\n            plan_name=subscription.plan\n        )\n    return {\"status\": \"success\", \"message\": \"Payment confirmed, provisioning site.\"}\n\n# -------------------------------\n# 5.
